76→\taddressType discovery.AddressType\n    77→}\n    78→\n    79→// Reconcile takes a set of pods currently matching a service selector and\n    80→// compares them with the endpoints already present in any existing endpoint\n    81→// slices for the given service. It creates, updates, or deletes endpoint slices\n    82→// to ensure the desired set of pods are represented by endpoint slices.\n    83→func (r *Reconciler) Reconcile(logger klog.Logger, service *corev1.Service, pods []*corev1.Pod, existingSlices []*discovery.EndpointSlice, triggerTime time.Time) error {\n    84→\tslicesToDelete := []*discovery.EndpointSlice{}                                    // slices that are no longer  matching any address the service has\n    85→\terrs := []error{}                                                                 // all errors generated in the process longer match address type supported by services\n    93→\t// go to delete, other slices goes to the Reconciler machinery\n    94→\t// for further adjustment\n    95→\tfor _, existingSlice := range type) for the given service. It creates, updates, or deletes endpoint slices\n   146→// to ensure the desired set of pods are represented by endpoint slices.\n   147→func (r *Reconciler) reconcileByAddressType(logger klog.Logger, 184→\t\t\t\tports:       endpointPorts,\n   185→\t\t\t}\n   186→\t\t}\n   187→\n   188→\t\tnode, err := r.nodeLister.Get(pod.Spec.NodeName)\n   189→\t\tif err != nil {\n   190→\t\t\t// we are getting 195→\t\t\t// If the Node specified by the Pod doesn't exist we want to requeue the Service so we\n   196→\t\t\t// retry later, but also update the EndpointSlice without the problematic Pod.\n   197→\t\t\t// Theoretically, the pod Garbage Collector will remove the Pod, but we want to avoid\n   198→\t\t\t// situations where a reference from a Pod to a missing node can leave the EndpointSlice\n   199→\t\t\t// stuck forever.\n   200→\t\t\t// On the other side, if the service.Spec.PublishNotReadyAddresses is set we just add the\n   201→\t\t\t// Pod, since the user is explicitly indicating that desiredEndpointsByPortMap {\n   220→\t\tnumEndpoints := len(desiredEndpoints)\n   221→\t\tpmSlicesToCreate, pmSlicesToUpdate, pmSlicesToDelete, added, removed := r.reconcileByPortMapping(\n   222→\t\t\tlogger, service, existingSlicesByPortMap[portMap], desiredEndpoints, desiredMetaByPortMap[portMap])\n   223→\n   224→\t\ttotalAdded += added\n   225→\t\ttotalRemoved += removed\n   226→\n   227→\t\tspMetrics.Set(portMap, metrics.EfficiencyInfo{\n   228→\t\t\tEndpoints: numEndpoints,\n   229→\t\t\tSlices:    len(existingSlicesByPortMap[portMap]) + len(pmSlicesToCreate) - len(pmSlicesToDelete),\n   230→\t\t})\n   231→\n   232→\t\tslicesToCreate = append(slicesToCreate, pmSlicesToCreate...)\n   233→\t\tslicesToUpdate = append(slicesToUpdate, pmSlicesToUpdate...)\n   234→\t\tslicesToDelete = append(slicesToDelete, pmSlicesToDelete...)\n   235→\t}\n   236→\n   237→\t// If there are unique sets of ports that are no longer desired, mark\n   238→\t// the corresponding endpoint slices for deletion.\n   239→\tfor portMap, existingSlices := range existingSlicesByPortMap {\n   240→\t\tif _, ok := desiredEndpointsByPortMap[portMap]; !ok {\n   241→\t\t\tslicesToDelete = append(slicesToDelete, existingSlices...)\n   242→\t\t}\n   243→\t}\n   244→\n   245→\t// When no endpoint slices would usually exist, we need to add a placeholder.\n   246→\tif len(existingSlices) == len(slicesToDelete) && len(slicesToCreate) < 1 {\n   247→\t\t// Check for existing placeholder slice outside of the core control flow\n   248→\t\tplaceholderSlice := newEndpointSlice(logger, service, &endpointMeta{ports: []discovery.EndpointPort{}, addressType: addressType}, r.controllerName)\n   249→\t\tif len(slicesToDelete) == 1 && placeholderSliceCompare.DeepEqual(slicesToDelete[0], placeholderSlice) {\n   250→\t\t\t// We are about to unnecessarily delete/recreate the placeholder, remove it now.\n   251→\t\t\tslicesToDelete = slicesToDelete[:0]\n   252→\t\t} else {\n   253→\t\t\tslicesToCreate = append(slicesToCreate, placeholderSlice)\n   254→\t\t}\n   255→\t\tspMetrics.Set(endpointsliceutil.NewPortMapKey(placeholderSlice.Ports), metrics.EfficiencyInfo{\n   256→\t\t\tEndpoints: 0,\n   257→\t\t\tSlices:    1,\n   258→\t\t})\n   259→\t}\n   260→\n   261→\tmetrics.EndpointsAddedPerSync.WithLabelValues().Observe(float64(totalAdded))\n   262→\tmetrics.EndpointsRemovedPerSync.WithLabelValues().Observe(float64(totalRemoved))\n   263→\n   264→\tserviceNN := types.NamespacedName{Name: service.Name, Namespace: service.Namespace}\n   265→\tr.metricsCache.UpdateServicePortCache(serviceNN, spMetrics)\n   266→\n   267→\t// Topology hints are assigned per address type. This means it is\n   268→\t// theoretically possible for endpoints of one address type to be assigned\n   269→\t// hints while another endpoints of another address type are not.\n   270→\tsi := &topologycache.SliceInfo{\n   271→\t\tServiceKey:  fmt.Sprintf(\"%s/%s\", service.Namespace, service.Name),\n   272→\t\tAddressType: addressType,\n   273→\t\tToCreate:    slicesToCreate,\n   274→\t\tToUpdate:    slicesToUpdate,\n   275→\t\tUnchanged:   unchangedSlices(existingSlices, slicesToUpdate, slicesToDelete),\n   276→\t}\n   277→\n   278→\tcanUseTrafficDistribution := r.trafficDistributionEnabled && !hintsEnabled(service.Annotations)\n   279→\n   280→\t// Check if we need to add/remove hints based on the topology annotation.\n   281→\t//\n   282→\t// This if/else clause can be removed once the annotation has been deprecated.\n   283→\t// Ref: https://github.com/kubernetes/enhancements/tree/master/keps/sig-network/4444-service-routing-preference\n   284→\tif r.topologyCache != nil && hintsEnabled(service.Annotations) {\n   285→\t\t// Reaching this point means that we need to configure hints based on the\n   286→\t\t// topology annotation.\n   287→\t\tslicesToCreate, slicesToUpdate, events = r.topologyCache.AddHints(logger, si)\n   288→\n   289→\t} else {\n   290→\t\t// Reaching this point means that we will not be configuring hints based on\n   291→\t\t// the topology annotation. We need to do 2 things:\n   292→\t\t//  1. If hints were added previously based on the annotation, we need to\n   293→\t\t//     clear up any locally cached hints from the topologyCache object.\n   294→\t\t//  2. Optionally remove the actual hints from the EndpointSlice if we know\n   295→\t\t//     that the `trafficDistribution` field is also NOT being used. In other\n   296→\t\t//     words, if we know that the `trafficDistribution` field has been\n   297→\t\t//     correctly configured by the customer, we DO NOT remove the hints and\n   298→\t\t//     wait for the trafficDist handlers to correctly configure them. Always\n   299→\t\t//     unconditionally removing hints here (and letting them get readded by\n   300→\t\t//     the trafficDist) adds extra overhead in the form of DeepCopy (done\n   301→\t\t//     within topologyCache.RemoveHints)\n   302→\n   303→\t\t// Check 1.\n   304→\t\tif r.topologyCache != nil {\n   305→\t\t\tif r.topologyCache.HasPopulatedHints(si.ServiceKey) {\n   306→\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"TopologyAwareHints annotation has changed, removing hints\", \"serviceKey\", si.ServiceKey, \"addressType\", si.AddressType)\n   307→\t\t\t\tevents = append(events, &topologycache.EventBuilder{\n   308→\t\t\t\t\tEventType: corev1.EventTypeWarning,\n   309→\t\t\t\t\tReason:    \"TopologyAwareHintsDisabled\",\n   310→\t\t\t\t\tMessage:   topologycache.FormatWithAddressType(topologycache.TopologyAwareHintsDisabled, si.AddressType),\n   311→\t\t\t\t})\n   312→\t\t\t}\n   313→\t\t\tr.topologyCache.RemoveHints(si.ServiceKey, addressType)\n   314→\t\t}\n   315→\n   316→\t\t// Check 2.\n   317→\t\tif !canUseTrafficDistribution {\n   318→\t\t\tslicesToCreate, slicesToUpdate = topologycache.RemoveHintsFromSlices(si)\n   319→\t\t}\n   320→\t}\n   321→\n   322→\tif canUseTrafficDistribution {\n   323→\t\tr.metricsCache.UpdateTrafficDistributionForService(serviceNN, service.Spec.TrafficDistribution)\n   324→\t\tslicesToCreate, slicesToUpdate, _ = trafficdist.ReconcileHints(service.Spec.TrafficDistribution, slicesToCreate, slicesToUpdate, unchangedSlices(existingSlices, slicesToUpdate, slicesToDelete))\n   325→\t} else {\n   326→\t\tr.metricsCache.UpdateTrafficDistributionForService(serviceNN, nil)\n   327→\t}\n   328→\n   329→\terr := r.finalize(service, slicesToCreate, slicesToUpdate, slicesToDelete, triggerTime)\n   330→\tif err != nil {\n   331→\t\terrs = append(errs, err)\n   332→\t}\n   333→\tfor _, event := range events {\n   334→\t\tr.eventRecorder.Event(service, event.EventType, event.Reason, event.Message)\n   335→\t}\n   336→\treturn utilerrors.NewAggregate(errs)\n   337→\n   338→}\n   339→\n   340→func NewReconciler(client clientset.Interface, nodeLister corelisters.NodeLister, maxEndpointsPerSlice int32, endpointSliceTracker *endpointsliceutil.EndpointSliceTracker, topologyCache *topologycache.TopologyCache, eventRecorder record.EventRecorder, controllerName string, options ...ReconcilerOption) *Reconciler {\n   341→\tr := &Reconciler{\n   342→\t\tclient:               client,\n   343→\t\tnodeLister:           nodeLister,\n   344→\t\tmaxEndpointsPerSlice: maxEndpointsPerSlice,\n   345→\t\tendpointSliceTracker: endpointSliceTracker,\n   346→\t\tmetricsCache:         metrics.NewCache(maxEndpointsPerSlice),\n   347→\t\ttopologyCache:        topologyCache,\n   348→\t\teventRecorder:        eventRecorder,\n   349→\t\tcontrollerName:       controllerName,\n   350→\t}\n   351→\tfor _, option := range options {\n   352→\t\toption(r)\n   353→\t}\n   354→\treturn r\n   355→}\n   356→\n   357→// placeholderSliceCompare is a conversion func for comparing two placeholder endpoint slices.\n   358→// It only compares the specific fields we care about.\n   359→var placeholderSliceCompare = conversion.EqualitiesOrDie(\n   360→\tfunc(a, b metav1.OwnerReference) bool {\n   361→\t\treturn a.String() == b.String()\n   362→\t},\n   363→\tfunc(a, b metav1.ObjectMeta) bool {\n   364→\t\tif a.Namespace != b.Namespace {\n   365→\t\t\treturn false\n   366→\t\t}\n   367→\t\tfor k, v := range a.Labels {\n   368→\t\t\tif b.Labels[k] != v {\n   369→\t\t\t\treturn false\n   370→\t\t\t}\n   371→\t\t}\n   372→\t\tfor k, v := range b.Labels {\n   373→\t\t\tif a.Labels[k] != v {\n   374→\t\t\t\treturn false\n   375→\t\t\t}\n   376→\t\t}\n   377→\t\treturn true\n   378→\t},\n   379→)\n   380→\n   381→// finalize creates, updates, and deletes slices as specified\n   382→func (r *Reconciler) finalize(\n   383→\tservice *corev1.Service,\n   384→\tslicesToCreate,\n   385→\tslicesToUpdate,\n   386→\tslicesToDelete []*discovery.EndpointSlice,\n   387→\ttriggerTime time.Time,\n   388→) error {\n   389→\t// If there are slices to create and delete, change the creates to updates\n   390→\t// of the slices that would otherwise be deleted.\n   391→\tfor i := 0; i < len(slicesToDelete); {\n   392→\t\tif len(slicesToCreate) == 0 {\n   393→\t\t\tbreak\n   394→\t\t}\n   395→\t\tsliceToDelete := slicesToDelete[i]\n   396→\t\tslice := slicesToCreate[len(slicesToCreate)-1]\n   397→\t\t// Only update EndpointSlices that are owned by this Service and have\n   398→\t\t// the same AddressType. We need to avoid updating EndpointSlices that\n   399→\t\t// are being garbage collected for an old Service with the same name.\n   400→\t\t// The AddressType field is immutable. Since Services also consider\n   401→\t\t// IPFamily immutable, the only case where this should matter will be\n   402→\t\t// the migration from IP to IPv4 and IPv6 AddressTypes, where there's a\n   403→\t\t// chance EndpointSlices with an IP AddressType would otherwise be\n   404→\t\t// updated to IPv4 or IPv6 without this check.\n   405→\t\tif sliceToDelete.AddressType == slice.AddressType && ownedBy(sliceToDelete, service) {\n   406→\t\t\tslice.Name = sliceToDelete.Name\n   407→\t\t\tslicesToCreate = slicesToCreate[:len(slicesToCreate)-1]\n   408→\t\t\tslicesToUpdate = append(slicesToUpdate, slice)\n   409→\t\t\tslicesToDelete = append(slicesToDelete[:i], slicesToDelete[i+1:]...)\n   410→\t\t} else {\n   411→\t\t\ti++\n   412→\t\t}\n   413→\t}\n   414→\n   415→\t// Don't create new EndpointSlices if the Service is pending deletion. This\n   416→\t// is to avoid a potential race condition with the garbage collector where\n   417→\t// it tries to delete EndpointSlices as this controller replaces them.\n   418→\tif service.DeletionTimestamp == nil {\n   419→\t\tfor _, endpointSlice := range slicesToCreate {\n   420→\t\t\taddTriggerTimeAnnotation(endpointSlice, triggerTime)\n   421→\t\t\tcreatedSlice, err := r.client.DiscoveryV1().EndpointSlices(service.Namespace).Create(context.TODO(), endpointSlice, metav1.CreateOptions{})\n   422→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   423→\t\t\t\t// If the namespace is terminating, creates will continue to fail. Simply drop the item.\n   424→\t\t\t\tif errors.HasStatusCause(err, corev1.NamespaceTerminatingCause) {\n   425→\t\t\t\t\treturn nil\n   426→\t\t\t\t}\n   427→\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to create EndpointSlice for Service %s/%s: %v\", service.Namespace, service.Name, err)\n   428→\t\t\t}\n   429→\t\t\tr.endpointSliceTracker.Update(createdSlice)\n   430→\t\t\tmetrics.EndpointSliceChanges.WithLabelValues(\"create\").Inc()\n   431→\t\t}\n   432→\t}\n   433→\n   434→\tfor _, endpointSlice := range slicesToUpdate {\n   435→\t\taddTriggerTimeAnnotation(endpointSlice, triggerTime)\n   436→\t\tupdatedSlice, err := r.client.DiscoveryV1().EndpointSlices(service.Namespace).Update(context.TODO(), endpointSlice, metav1.UpdateOptions{})\n   437→\t\tif err != nil {\n   438→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to update %s EndpointSlice for Service %s/%s: %v\", endpointSlice.Name, service.Namespace, service.Name, err)\n   439→\t\t}\n   440→\t\tr.endpointSliceTracker.Update(updatedSlice)\n   441→\t\tmetrics.EndpointSliceChanges.WithLabelValues(\"update\").Inc()\n   442→\t}\n   443→\n   444→\tfor _, endpointSlice := range slicesToDelete {\n   445→\t\terr := r.client.DiscoveryV1().EndpointSlices(service.Namespace).Delete(context.TODO(), endpointSlice.Name, metav1.DeleteOptions{})\n   446→\t\tif err != nil {\n   447→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to delete %s EndpointSlice for Service %s/%s: %v\", endpointSlice.Name, service.Namespace, service.Name, err)\n   448→\t\t}\n   449→\t\tr.endpointSliceTracker.ExpectDeletion(endpointSlice)\n   450→\t\tmetrics.EndpointSliceChanges.WithLabelValues(\"delete\").Inc()\n   451→\t}\n   452→\n   453→\ttopologyLabel := \"Disabled\"\n   454→\tif r.topologyCache != nil && hintsEnabled(service.Annotations) {\n   455→\t\ttopologyLabel = \"Auto\"\n   456→\t}\n   457→\tvar trafficDistribution string\n   458→\tif r.trafficDistributionEnabled && !hintsEnabled(service.Annotations) {\n   459→\t\tif service.Spec.TrafficDistribution != nil && *service.Spec.TrafficDistribution == corev1.ServiceTrafficDistributionPreferClose {\n   460→\t\t\ttrafficDistribution = *service.Spec.TrafficDistribution\n   461→\t\t}\n   462→\t}\n   463→\n   464→\tnumSlicesChanged := len(slicesToCreate) + len(slicesToUpdate) + len(slicesToDelete)\n   465→\tmetrics.EndpointSlicesChangedPerSync.WithLabelValues(topologyLabel, trafficDistribution).Observe(float64(numSlicesChanged))\n   466→\n   467→\treturn nil\n   468→}\n   469→\n   470→// reconcileByPortMapping compares the endpoints found in existing slices with\n   471→// the list of desired endpoints and returns lists of slices to create, update,\n   472→// and delete. It also checks that the slices mirror the parent services labels.\n   473→// The logic is split up into several main steps:\n   474→//  1. Iterate through existing slices, delete endpoints that are no longer\n   475→//     desired and update matching endpoints that have changed. It also checks\n   476→//     if the slices have the labels of the parent services, and updates them if not.\n   477→//  2. Iterate through slices that have been modified in 1 and fill them up with\n   478→//     any remaining desired endpoints.\n   479→//  3. If there still desired endpoints left, try to fit them into a previously\n   480→//     unchanged slice and/or create new ones.\n   481→func (r *Reconciler) reconcileByPortMapping(\n   482→\tlogger klog.Logger,\n   483→\tservice *corev1.Service,\n   484→\texistingSlices []*discovery.EndpointSlice,\n   485→\tdesiredSet endpointsliceutil.EndpointSet,\n   486→\tendpointMeta *endpointMeta,\n   487→) ([]*discovery.EndpointSlice, []*discovery.EndpointSlice, []*discovery.EndpointSlice, int, int) {\n   488→\tslicesByName := map[string]*discovery.EndpointSlice{}\n   489→\tsliceNamesUnchanged := sets.New[string]()\n   490→\tsliceNamesToUpdate := sets.New[string]()\n   491→\tsliceNamesToDelete := sets.New[string]()\n   492→\tnumRemoved := 0\n   493→\n   494→\t// 1. Iterate through existing slices to delete endpoints no longer desired\n   495→\t//    and update endpoints that have changed\n   496→\tfor _, existingSlice := range existingSlices {\n   497→\t\tslicesByName[existingSlice.Name] = existingSlice\n   498→\t\tnewEndpoints := []discovery.Endpoint{}\n   499→\t\tendpointUpdated := false\n   500→\t\tfor _, endpoint := range existingSlice.Endpoints {\n   501→\t\t\tgot := desiredSet.Get(&endpoint)\n   502→\t\t\t// If endpoint is desired add it to list of endpoints to keep.\n   503→\t\t\tif got != nil {\n   504→\t\t\t\tnewEndpoints = append(newEndpoints, *got)\n   505→\t\t\t\t// If existing version of endpoint doesn't match desired version\n   506→\t\t\t\t// set endpointUpdated to ensure endpoint changes are persisted.\n   507→\t\t\t\tif !endpointsliceutil.EndpointsEqualBeyondHash(got, &endpoint) {\n   508→\t\t\t\t\tendpointUpdated = true\n   509→\t\t\t\t}\n   510→\t\t\t\t// once an endpoint has been placed/found in a slice, it no\n   511→\t\t\t\t// longer needs to be handled\n   512→\t\t\t\tdesiredSet.Delete(&endpoint)\n   513→\t\t\t}\n   514→\t\t}\n   515→\n   516→\t\t// generate the slice labels and check if parent labels have changed\n   517→\t\tlabels, labelsChanged := setEndpointSliceLabels(logger, existingSlice, service, r.controllerName)\n   518→\n   519→\t\t// If an endpoint was updated or removed, mark for update or delete\n   520→\t\tif endpointUpdated || len(existingSlice.Endpoints) != len(newEndpoints) {\n   521→\t\t\tif len(existingSlice.Endpoints) > len(newEndpoints) {\n   522→\t\t\t\tnumRemoved += len(existingSlice.Endpoints) - len(newEndpoints)\n   523→\t\t\t}\n   524→\t\t\tif len(newEndpoints) == 0 {\n   525→\t\t\t\t// if no endpoints desired in this slice, mark for deletion\n   526→\t\t\t\tsliceNamesToDelete.Insert(existingSlice.Name)\n   527→\t\t\t} else {\n   528→\t\t\t\t// otherwise, copy and mark for update\n   529→\t\t\t\tepSlice := existingSlice.DeepCopy()\n   530→\t\t\t\tepSlice.Endpoints = newEndpoints\n   531→\t\t\t\tepSlice.Labels = labels\n   532→\t\t\t\tslicesByName[existingSlice.Name] = epSlice\n   533→\t\t\t\tsliceNamesToUpdate.Insert(epSlice.Name)\n   534→\t\t\t}\n   535→\t\t} else if labelsChanged {\n   536→\t\t\t// if labels have changed, copy and mark for update\n   537→\t\t\tepSlice := existingSlice.DeepCopy()\n   538→\t\t\tepSlice.Labels = labels\n   539→\t\t\tslicesByName[existingSlice.Name] = epSlice\n   540→\t\t\tsliceNamesToUpdate.Insert(epSlice.Name)\n   541→\t\t} else {\n   542→\t\t\t// slices with no changes will be useful if there are leftover endpoints\n   543→\t\t\tsliceNamesUnchanged.Insert(existingSlice.Name)\n   544→\t\t}\n   545→\t}\n   546→\n   547→\tnumAdded := desiredSet.Len()\n   548→\n   549→\t// 2. If we still have desired endpoints to add and slices marked for update,\n   550→\t//    iterate through the slices and fill them up with the desired endpoints.\n   551→\tif desiredSet.Len() > 0 && sliceNamesToUpdate.Len() > 0 {\n   552→\t\tslices := []*discovery.EndpointSlice{}\n   553→\t\tfor _, sliceName := range sliceNamesToUpdate.UnsortedList() {\n   554→\t\t\tslices = append(slices, slicesByName[sliceName])\n   555→\t\t}\n   556→\t\t// Sort endpoint slices by length so we're filling up the fullest ones\n   557→\t\t// first.\n   558→\t\tsort.Sort(endpointSliceEndpointLen(slices))\n   559→\n   560→\t\t// Iterate through slices and fill them up with desired endpoints.\n   561→\t\tfor _, slice := range slices {\n   562→\t\t\tfor desiredSet.Len() > 0 && len(slice.Endpoints) < int(r.maxEndpointsPerSlice) {\n   563→\t\t\t\tendpoint, _ := desiredSet.PopAny()\n   564→\t\t\t\tslice.Endpoints = append(slice.Endpoints, *endpoint)\n   565→\t\t\t}\n   566→\t\t}\n   567→\t}\n   568→\n   569→\t// 3. If there are still desired endpoints left at this point, we try to fit\n   570→\t//    the endpoints in a single existing slice. If there are no slices with\n   571→\t//    that capacity, we create new slices for the endpoints.\n   572→\tslicesToCreate := []*discovery.EndpointSlice{}\n   573→\n   574→\tfor desiredSet.Len() > 0 {\n   575→\t\tvar sliceToFill *discovery.EndpointSlice\n   576→\n   577→\t\t// If the remaining amounts of endpoints is smaller than the max\n   578→\t\t// endpoints per slice and we have slices that haven't already been\n   579→\t\t// filled, try to fit them in one.\n   580→\t\tif desiredSet.Len() < int(r.maxEndpointsPerSlice) && sliceNamesUnchanged.Len() > 0 {\n   581→\t\t\tunchangedSlices := []*discovery.EndpointSlice{}\n   582→\t\t\tfor _, sliceName := range sliceNamesUnchanged.UnsortedList() {\n   583→\t\t\t\tunchangedSlices = append(unchangedSlices, slicesByName[sliceName])\n   584→\t\t\t}\n   585→\t\t\tsliceToFill = getSliceToFill(unchangedSlices, desiredSet.Len(), int(r.maxEndpointsPerSlice))\n   586→\t\t}\n   587→\n   588→\t\t// If we didn't find a sliceToFill, generate a new empty one.\n   589→\t\tif sliceToFill == nil {\n   590→\t\t\tsliceToFill = newEndpointSlice(logger, service, endpointMeta, r.controllerName)\n   591→\t\t} else {\n   592→\t\t\t// deep copy required to modify this slice.\n   593→\t\t\tsliceToFill = sliceToFill.DeepCopy()\n   594→\t\t\tslicesByName[sliceToFill.Name] = sliceToFill\n   595→\t\t}\n   596→\n   597→\t\t// Fill the slice up with remaining endpoints.\n   598→\t\tfor desiredSet.Len() > 0 && len(sliceToFill.Endpoints) < int(r.maxEndpointsPerSlice) {\n   599→\t\t\tendpoint, _ := desiredSet.PopAny()\n   600→\t\t\tsliceToFill.Endpoints = append(sliceToFill.Endpoints, *endpoint)\n   601→\t\t}\n   602→\n   603→\t\t// New slices will not have a Name set, use this to determine whether\n   604→\t\t// this should be an update or create.\n   605→\t\tif sliceToFill.Name != \"\" {\n   606→\t\t\tsliceNamesToUpdate.Insert(sliceToFill.Name)\n   607→\t\t\tsliceNamesUnchanged.Delete(sliceToFill.Name)\n   608→\t\t} else {\n   609→\t\t\tslicesToCreate = append(slicesToCreate, sliceToFill)\n   610→\t\t}\n   611→\t}\n   612→\n   613→\t// Build slicesToUpdate from slice names.\n   614→\tslicesToUpdate := []*discovery.EndpointSlice{}\n   615→\tfor _, sliceName := range sliceNamesToUpdate.UnsortedList() {\n   616→\t\tslicesToUpdate = append(slicesToUpdate, slicesByName[sliceName])\n   617→\t}\n   618→\n   619→\t// Build slicesToDelete from slice names.\n   620→\tslicesToDelete := []*discovery.EndpointSlice{}\n   621→\tfor _, sliceName := range sliceNamesToDelete.UnsortedList() {\n   622→\t\tslicesToDelete = append(slicesToDelete, slicesByName[sliceName])\n   623→\t}\n   624→\n   625→\treturn slicesToCreate, slicesToUpdate, slicesToDelete, numAdded, numRemoved\n   626→}\n   627→\n   628→func (r *Reconciler) DeleteService(namespace, name string) {\n   629→\tr.metricsCache.DeleteService(types.NamespacedName{Namespace: namespace, Name: name})\n   630→}\n   631→\n   632→func (r *Reconciler) GetControllerName() string {\n   633→\treturn r.controllerName\n   634→}\n   635→\n   636→// ManagedByChanged returns true if one of the provided EndpointSlices is\n   637→// managed by the EndpointSlice controller while the other is not.\n   638→func (r *Reconciler) ManagedByChanged(endpointSlice1, endpointSlice2 *discovery.EndpointSlice) bool {\n   639→\treturn r.ManagedByController(endpointSlice1) != r.ManagedByController(endpointSlice2)\n   640→}\n   641→\n   642→// ManagedByController returns true if the controller of the provided\n   643→// EndpointSlices is the EndpointSlice controller.\n   644→func (r *Reconciler) ManagedByController(endpointSlice *discovery.EndpointSlice) bool {\n   645→\tmanagedBy := endpointSlice.Labels[discovery.LabelManagedBy]\n   646→\treturn managedBy == r.controllerName\n   647→}\n   648→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. \"k8s.io/endpointslice/util\"\n\t\"k8s.io/klog/v2\"\n)\n\n// Reconciler is responsible for transforming current EndpointSlice state into\n// desired state\ntype Reconciler struct {\n\tclient It creates, updates, or deletes endpoint slices\n// to ensure the desired set of pods are represented by endpoint slices.\nfunc (r *Reconciler) Reconcile(logger klog.Logger, service *corev1.Service, pods []*corev1.Pod, existingSlices []*discovery.EndpointSlice, triggerTime time.Time) error {\n\tslicesToDelete := []*discovery.EndpointSlice{}                                    // slices that are no longer  matching any address the service has\n\terrs := []error{}                                                                 // all errors generated in the process of reconciling\n\tslicesByAddressType := make(map[discovery.AddressType][]*discovery.EndpointSlice) // slices by address type\n\n\t// addresses that this service supports [o(1) find]\n\tserviceSupportedAddressesTypes := getAddressTypesForService(logger, service)\n\n\t// loop through slices identifying their address type.\n\t// slices that no longer match address type supported by services\n\t// go to delete, other slices goes to the Reconciler machinery\n\t// for further adjustment\n\tfor _, existingSlice := range existingSlices {\n\t\t// service no longer supports that address type, add it to deleted slices\n\t\tif !serviceSupportedAddressesTypes.Has(existingSlice.AddressType) {\n\t\t\tif r.topologyCache != nil {\n\t\t\t\tsvcKey, err := ServiceControllerKey(existingSlice)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"Couldn't get key to remove EndpointSlice from topology cache\", \"existingSlice\", existingSlice, \"err\", err)\n\t\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t\tr.topologyCache.RemoveHints(svcKey, existingSlice.AddressType)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tslicesToDelete = append(slicesToDelete, existingSlice)\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// add list if it is not on our map\n\t\tif _, ok := slicesByAddressType[existingSlice.AddressType]; !ok {\n\t\t\tslicesByAddressType[existingSlice.AddressType] = make([]*discovery.EndpointSlice, 0, 1)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tslicesByAddressType[existingSlice.AddressType] = append(slicesByAddressType[existingSlice.AddressType], existingSlice)\n\t}\n\n\t// reconcile for existing.\n\tfor addressType := range serviceSupportedAddressesTypes {\n\t\texistingSlices := slicesByAddressType[addressType]\n\t\terr := r.reconcileByAddressType(logger, service, pods, existingSlices, triggerTime, addressType)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\terrs = append(errs, err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// delete those which are of addressType that is no longer supported\n\t// by the service\n\tfor _, sliceToDelete := range slicesToDelete {\n\t\terr := r.client.DiscoveryV1().EndpointSlices(service.Namespace).Delete(context.TODO(), sliceToDelete.Name, metav1.DeleteOptions{})\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\terrs = append(errs, fmt.Errorf(\"error deleting %s EndpointSlice for Service %s/%s: %w\", sliceToDelete.Name, service.Namespace, service.Name, err))\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tr.endpointSliceTracker.ExpectDeletion(sliceToDelete)\n\t\t\tmetrics.EndpointSliceChanges.WithLabelValues(\"delete\").Inc()\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn utilerrors.NewAggregate(errs)\n}\n\n// reconcileByAddressType takes a set of pods currently matching a service selector and\n// compares them with the endpoints already present in any existing endpoint\n// slices (by address type) for the given service. - len(pmSlicesToDelete),\n\t\t})\n\n\t\tslicesToCreate = append(slicesToCreate, pmSlicesToCreate...)\n\t\tslicesToUpdate = append(slicesToUpdate, pmSlicesToUpdate...)\n\t\tslicesToDelete = of the core control flow\n\t\tplaceholderSlice := newEndpointSlice(logger, service, &endpointMeta{ports: []discovery.EndpointPort{}, addressType: addressType}, r.controllerName)\n\t\tif len(slicesToDelete) == 1 && placeholderSliceCompare.DeepEqual(slicesToDelete[0], placeholderSlice) {\n\t\t\t// We are about to unnecessarily delete/recreate the placeholder, remove it now.\n\t\t\tslicesToDelete = slicesToDelete[:0]\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tslicesToCreate = append(slicesToCreate, placeholderSlice)\n\t\t}\n\t\tspMetrics.Set(endpointsliceutil.NewPortMapKey(placeholderSlice.Ports), metrics.EfficiencyInfo{\n\t\t\tEndpoints: 0,\n\t\t\tSlices:    1,\n\t\t})\n\t}\n\n\tmetrics.EndpointsAddedPerSync.WithLabelValues().Observe(float64(totalAdded))\n\tmetrics.EndpointsRemovedPerSync.WithLabelValues().Observe(float64(totalRemoved))\n\n\tserviceNN := This means it is\n\t// theoretically possible for endpoints of one address type to be assigned\n\t// hints while another endpoints of another address type are not.\n\tsi := &topologycache.SliceInfo{\n\t\tServiceKey:  fmt.Sprintf(\"%s/%s\", service.Namespace, service.Name),\n\t\tAddressType: addressType,\n\t\tToCreate:    slicesToCreate,\n\t\tToUpdate:    slicesToUpdate,\n\t\tUnchanged:   unchangedSlices(existingSlices, slicesToUpdate, slicesToDelete),\n\t}\n\n\tcanUseTrafficDistribution := r.trafficDistributionEnabled && !hintsEnabled(service.Annotations)\n\n\t// Check if we need to add/remove hints based on the topology annotation.\n\t//\n\t// This if/else clause can be removed once the annotation has been deprecated.\n\t// Ref: https://github.com/kubernetes/enhancements/tree/master/keps/sig-network/4444-service-routing-preference\n\tif r.topologyCache != nil && hintsEnabled(service.Annotations) {\n\t\t// Reaching this point means that we need to configure hints based on the\n\t\t// topology annotation.\n\t\tslicesToCreate, slicesToUpdate, events = r.topologyCache.AddHints(logger, si)\n\n\t} else {\n\t\t// Reaching this point means that we will not be configuring hints based on\n\t\t// the topology annotation. We need to do 2 things:\n\t\t//  1. If hints were added previously based on the annotation, we need to\n\t\t//     clear up any locally cached hints from the topologyCache object.\n\t\t//  2. Optionally remove the actual hints from the EndpointSlice if we know\n\t\t//     that the `trafficDistribution` field is also NOT being used. In other\n\t\t//     words, if we know that the `trafficDistribution` field has been\n\t\t//     correctly configured by the customer, we DO NOT remove the hints and\n\t\t//     wait for the trafficDist handlers to correctly configure them. Always\n\t\t//     unconditionally removing hints here (and letting them get readded by\n\t\t//     the trafficDist) adds extra overhead in the form of DeepCopy (done\n\t\t//     within topologyCache.RemoveHints)\n\n\t\t// Check 1.\n\t\tif r.topologyCache != nil {\n\t\t\tif r.topologyCache.HasPopulatedHints(si.ServiceKey) {\n\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"TopologyAwareHints annotation has changed, removing hints\", \"serviceKey\", si.ServiceKey, \"addressType\", si.AddressType)\n\t\t\t\tevents = append(events, &topologycache.EventBuilder{\n\t\t\t\t\tEventType: corev1.EventTypeWarning,\n\t\t\t\t\tReason:    \"TopologyAwareHintsDisabled\",\n\t\t\t\t\tMessage:   topologycache.FormatWithAddressType(topologycache.TopologyAwareHintsDisabled, si.AddressType),\n\t\t\t\t})\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tr.topologyCache.RemoveHints(si.ServiceKey, addressType)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Check 2.\n\t\tif !canUseTrafficDistribution {\n\t\t\tslicesToCreate, slicesToUpdate = topologycache.RemoveHintsFromSlices(si)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif canUseTrafficDistribution {\n\t\tr.metricsCache.UpdateTrafficDistributionForService(serviceNN, service.Spec.TrafficDistribution)\n\t\tslicesToCreate, slicesToUpdate, _ = trafficdist.ReconcileHints(service.Spec.TrafficDistribution, slicesToCreate, slicesToUpdate, unchangedSlices(existingSlices, slicesToUpdate, slicesToDelete))\n\t} else {\n\t\tr.metricsCache.UpdateTrafficDistributionForService(serviceNN, nil)\n\t}\n\n\terr := r.finalize(service, slicesToCreate, slicesToUpdate, slicesToDelete, triggerTime)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\terrs = append(errs, err)\n\t}\n\tfor _, event := range events {\n\t\tr.eventRecorder.Event(service, event.EventType, event.Reason, event.Message)\n\t}\n\treturn utilerrors.NewAggregate(errs)\n\n}\n\nfunc NewReconciler(client clientset.Interface, nodeLister corelisters.NodeLister, maxEndpointsPerSlice int32, endpointSliceTracker *endpointsliceutil.EndpointSliceTracker, topologyCache *topologycache.TopologyCache, eventRecorder record.EventRecorder, controllerName string, options ...ReconcilerOption) *Reconciler {\n\tr := &Reconciler{\n\t\tclient:               client,\n\t\tnodeLister:           nodeLister,\n\t\tmaxEndpointsPerSlice: maxEndpointsPerSlice,\n\t\tendpointSliceTracker: endpointSliceTracker,\n\t\tmetricsCache:         metrics.NewCache(maxEndpointsPerSlice),\n\t\ttopologyCache:        topologyCache,\n\t\teventRecorder:        eventRecorder,\n\t\tcontrollerName:       controllerName,\n\t}\n\tfor _, option := range options {\n\t\toption(r)\n\t}\n\treturn r\n}\n\n// placeholderSliceCompare is a conversion func for comparing two placeholder endpoint slices.\n// It only compares the specific fields we care about.\nvar placeholderSliceCompare = conversion.EqualitiesOrDie(\n\tfunc(a, b metav1.OwnerReference) bool {\n\t\treturn a.String() == b.String()\n\t},\n\tfunc(a, b metav1.ObjectMeta) bool {\n\t\tif a.Namespace != b.Namespace {\n\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t}\n\t\tfor k, v := range a.Labels {\n\t\t\tif b.Labels[k] != v {\n\t\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\tfor k, v := range b.Labels {\n\t\t\tif a.Labels[k] != v {\n\t\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn true\n\t},\n)\n\n// finalize creates, updates, and deletes slices as specified\nfunc (r *Reconciler) finalize(\n\tservice *corev1.Service,\n\tslicesToCreate,\n\tslicesToUpdate,\n\tslicesToDelete []*discovery.EndpointSlice,\n\ttriggerTime time.Time,\n) error {\n\t// If there are slices to create and delete, change the creates to updates\n\t// of the slices that would otherwise be deleted.\n\tfor i := 0; i < len(slicesToDelete); {\n\t\tif len(slicesToCreate) == 0 {\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t\tsliceToDelete := slicesToDelete[i]\n\t\tslice := slicesToCreate[len(slicesToCreate)-1]\n\t\t// Only update EndpointSlices that are owned by this Service and have\n\t\t// the same AddressType. We need to avoid updating EndpointSlices that\n\t\t// are being garbage collected for an old Service with the same name.\n\t\t// The AddressType field is immutable. Since Services also consider\n\t\t// IPFamily immutable, the only case where this should matter will be\n\t\t// the migration from IP to IPv4 and IPv6 AddressTypes, where there's a\n\t\t// chance EndpointSlices with an IP AddressType would otherwise be\n\t\t// updated to IPv4 or IPv6 without this check.\n\t\tif sliceToDelete.AddressType == slice.AddressType && ownedBy(sliceToDelete, service) {\n\t\t\tslice.Name = sliceToDelete.Name\n\t\t\tslicesToCreate = slicesToCreate[:len(slicesToCreate)-1]\n\t\t\tslicesToUpdate = append(slicesToUpdate, slice)\n\t\t\tslicesToDelete = append(slicesToDelete[:i], slicesToDelete[i+1:]...)\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\ti++\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Don't create new EndpointSlices if the Service is pending deletion. This\n\t// is to avoid a potential race condition with the garbage collector where\n\t// it tries to delete EndpointSlices as this controller replaces them.\n\tif service.DeletionTimestamp == nil {\n\t\tfor _, endpointSlice := range slicesToCreate {\n\t\t\taddTriggerTimeAnnotation(endpointSlice, triggerTime)\n\t\t\tcreatedSlice, err := r.client.DiscoveryV1().EndpointSlices(service.Namespace).Create(context.TODO(), endpointSlice, metav1.CreateOptions{})\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t// If the namespace is terminating, creates will continue to fail. Simply drop the item.\n\t\t\t\tif errors.HasStatusCause(err, corev1.NamespaceTerminatingCause) {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to create EndpointSlice for Service %s/%s: %v\", service.Namespace, service.Name, err)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tr.endpointSliceTracker.Update(createdSlice)\n\t\t\tmetrics.EndpointSliceChanges.WithLabelValues(\"create\").Inc()\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, endpointSlice := range slicesToUpdate {\n\t\taddTriggerTimeAnnotation(endpointSlice, triggerTime)\n\t\tupdatedSlice, err := r.client.DiscoveryV1().EndpointSlices(service.Namespace).Update(context.TODO(), endpointSlice, metav1.UpdateOptions{})\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to update %s EndpointSlice for Service %s/%s: %v\", endpointSlice.Name, service.Namespace, service.Name, err)\n\t\t}\n\t\tr.endpointSliceTracker.Update(updatedSlice)\n\t\tmetrics.EndpointSliceChanges.WithLabelValues(\"update\").Inc()\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, endpointSlice := range slicesToDelete {\n\t\terr := r.client.DiscoveryV1().EndpointSlices(service.Namespace).Delete(context.TODO(), endpointSlice.Name, metav1.DeleteOptions{})\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to delete %s EndpointSlice for Service %s/%s: %v\", endpointSlice.Name, service.Namespace, service.Name, err)\n\t\t}\n\t\tr.endpointSliceTracker.ExpectDeletion(endpointSlice)\n\t\tmetrics.EndpointSliceChanges.WithLabelValues(\"delete\").Inc()\n\t}\n\n\ttopologyLabel := \"Disabled\"\n\tif r.topologyCache != nil && hintsEnabled(service.Annotations) {\n\t\ttopologyLabel = \"Auto\"\n\t}\n\tvar trafficDistribution string\n\tif r.trafficDistributionEnabled && !hintsEnabled(service.Annotations) {\n\t\tif service.Spec.TrafficDistribution != nil && *service.Spec.TrafficDistribution == corev1.ServiceTrafficDistributionPreferClose {\n\t\t\ttrafficDistribution = *service.Spec.TrafficDistribution\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tnumSlicesChanged := len(slicesToCreate) + len(slicesToUpdate) + len(slicesToDelete)\n\tmetrics.EndpointSlicesChangedPerSync.WithLabelValues(topologyLabel, trafficDistribution).Observe(float64(numSlicesChanged))\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// reconcileByPortMapping compares the endpoints found in existing slices with\n// the list of desired endpoints and returns lists of slices to create, update,\n// and delete. It also checks that the slices mirror the parent services labels.\n// The logic is split up into several main steps:\n//  1. Iterate through existing slices, delete endpoints that are no longer\n//     desired and update matching endpoints that have changed. It also checks\n//     if the slices have the labels of the parent services, and updates them if not.\n//  2. Iterate through slices that have been modified in 1 and fill them up with\n//     any remaining desired endpoints.\n//  3. If there still desired endpoints left, try to fit them into a previously\n//     unchanged slice and/or create new ones.\nfunc (r *Reconciler) reconcileByPortMapping(\n\tlogger klog.Logger,\n\tservice *corev1.Service,\n\texistingSlices []*discovery.EndpointSlice,\n\tdesiredSet endpointsliceutil.EndpointSet,\n\tendpointMeta *endpointMeta,\n) ([]*discovery.EndpointSlice, []*discovery.EndpointSlice, []*discovery.EndpointSlice, int, int) {\n\tslicesByName := map[string]*discovery.EndpointSlice{}\n\tsliceNamesUnchanged := sets.New[string]()\n\tsliceNamesToUpdate := sets.New[string]()\n\tsliceNamesToDelete := sets.New[string]()\n\tnumRemoved := 0\n\n\t// 1. Iterate through existing slices to delete endpoints no longer desired\n\t//    and update endpoints that have changed\n\tfor _, existingSlice := range existingSlices {\n\t\tslicesByName[existingSlice.Name] = existingSlice\n\t\tnewEndpoints := []discovery.Endpoint{}\n\t\tendpointUpdated := false\n\t\tfor _, endpoint := range existingSlice.Endpoints {\n\t\t\tgot := desiredSet.Get(&endpoint)\n\t\t\t// If endpoint is desired add it to list of endpoints to keep.\n\t\t\tif got != nil {\n\t\t\t\tnewEndpoints = append(newEndpoints, *got)\n\t\t\t\t// If existing version of endpoint doesn't match desired version\n\t\t\t\t// set endpointUpdated to ensure endpoint changes are persisted.\n\t\t\t\tif !endpointsliceutil.EndpointsEqualBeyondHash(got, &endpoint) {\n\t\t\t\t\tendpointUpdated = true\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t// once an endpoint has been placed/found in a slice, it no\n\t\t\t\t// longer needs to be handled\n\t\t\t\tdesiredSet.Delete(&endpoint)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// generate the slice labels and check if parent labels have changed\n\t\tlabels, labelsChanged := setEndpointSliceLabels(logger, existingSlice, service, r.controllerName)\n\n\t\t// If an endpoint was updated or removed, mark for update or delete\n\t\tif endpointUpdated || len(existingSlice.Endpoints) != len(newEndpoints) {\n\t\t\tif len(existingSlice.Endpoints) > len(newEndpoints) {\n\t\t\t\tnumRemoved += len(existingSlice.Endpoints) - len(newEndpoints)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif len(newEndpoints) == 0 {\n\t\t\t\t// if no endpoints desired in this slice, mark for deletion\n\t\t\t\tsliceNamesToDelete.Insert(existingSlice.Name)\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t// otherwise, copy and mark for update\n\t\t\t\tepSlice := existingSlice.DeepCopy()\n\t\t\t\tepSlice.Endpoints = newEndpoints\n\t\t\t\tepSlice.Labels = labels\n\t\t\t\tslicesByName[existingSlice.Name] = epSlice\n\t\t\t\tsliceNamesToUpdate.Insert(epSlice.Name)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t} else if labelsChanged {\n\t\t\t// if labels have changed, copy and mark for update\n\t\t\tepSlice := existingSlice.DeepCopy()\n\t\t\tepSlice.Labels = labels\n\t\t\tslicesByName[existingSlice.Name] = epSlice\n\t\t\tsliceNamesToUpdate.Insert(epSlice.Name)\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t// slices with no changes will be useful if there are leftover endpoints\n\t\t\tsliceNamesUnchanged.Insert(existingSlice.Name)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tnumAdded := desiredSet.Len()\n\n\t// 2. If we still have desired endpoints to add and slices marked for update,\n\t//    iterate through the slices and fill them up with the desired endpoints.\n\tif desiredSet.Len() > 0 && sliceNamesToUpdate.Len() > 0 {\n\t\tslices := []*discovery.EndpointSlice{}\n\t\tfor _, sliceName := range sliceNamesToUpdate.UnsortedList() {\n\t\t\tslices = append(slices, slicesByName[sliceName])\n\t\t}\n\t\t// Sort endpoint slices by length so we're filling up the fullest ones\n\t\t// first.\n\t\tsort.Sort(endpointSliceEndpointLen(slices))\n\n\t\t// Iterate through slices and fill them up with desired endpoints.\n\t\tfor _, slice := range slices {\n\t\t\tfor desiredSet.Len() > 0 && len(slice.Endpoints) < int(r.maxEndpointsPerSlice) {\n\t\t\t\tendpoint, _ := desiredSet.PopAny()\n\t\t\t\tslice.Endpoints = append(slice.Endpoints, *endpoint)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// 3. If there are still desired endpoints left at this point, we try to fit\n\t//    the endpoints in a single existing slice. If there are no slices with\n\t//    that capacity, we create new slices for the endpoints.\n\tslicesToCreate := []*discovery.EndpointSlice{}\n\n\tfor desiredSet.Len() > 0 {\n\t\tvar sliceToFill *discovery.EndpointSlice\n\n\t\t// If the remaining amounts of endpoints is smaller than the max\n\t\t// endpoints per slice and we have slices that haven't already been\n\t\t// filled, try to fit them in one.\n\t\tif desiredSet.Len() < int(r.maxEndpointsPerSlice) && sliceNamesUnchanged.Len() > 0 {\n\t\t\tunchangedSlices := []*discovery.EndpointSlice{}\n\t\t\tfor _, sliceName := range sliceNamesUnchanged.UnsortedList() {\n\t\t\t\tunchangedSlices = append(unchangedSlices, slicesByName[sliceName])\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tsliceToFill = getSliceToFill(unchangedSlices, desiredSet.Len(), int(r.maxEndpointsPerSlice))\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// If we didn't find a sliceToFill, generate a new empty one.\n\t\tif sliceToFill == nil {\n\t\t\tsliceToFill = newEndpointSlice(logger, service, endpointMeta, r.controllerName)\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t// deep copy required to modify this slice.\n\t\t\tsliceToFill = sliceToFill.DeepCopy()\n\t\t\tslicesByName[sliceToFill.Name] = sliceToFill\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Fill the slice up with remaining endpoints.\n\t\tfor desiredSet.Len() > 0 && len(sliceToFill.Endpoints) < int(r.maxEndpointsPerSlice) {\n\t\t\tendpoint, _ := desiredSet.PopAny()\n\t\t\tsliceToFill.Endpoints = append(sliceToFill.Endpoints, *endpoint)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// New slices will not have a Name set, use this to determine whether\n\t\t// this should be an update or create.\n\t\tif sliceToFill.Name != \"\" {\n\t\t\tsliceNamesToUpdate.Insert(sliceToFill.Name)\n\t\t\tsliceNamesUnchanged.Delete(sliceToFill.Name)\n\t\t} else {\n\t\t\tslicesToCreate = append(slicesToCreate, sliceToFill)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Build slicesToUpdate from slice names.\n\tslicesToUpdate := []*discovery.EndpointSlice{}\n\tfor _, sliceName := range sliceNamesToUpdate.UnsortedList() {\n\t\tslicesToUpdate = append(slicesToUpdate, slicesByName[sliceName])\n\t}\n\n\t// Build slicesToDelete from slice names.\n\tslicesToDelete := []*discovery.EndpointSlice{}\n\tfor _, sliceName := range sliceNamesToDelete.UnsortedList() {\n\t\tslicesToDelete = append(slicesToDelete, slicesByName[sliceName])\n\t}\n\n\treturn slicesToCreate, slicesToUpdate, slicesToDelete, numAdded, numRemoved\n}\n\nfunc (r *Reconciler) DeleteService(namespace, name string) {\n\tr.metricsCache.DeleteService(types.NamespacedName{Namespace: namespace, Name: name})\n}\n\nfunc (r *Reconciler) GetControllerName() string {\n\treturn r.controllerName\n}\n\n// ManagedByChanged returns true if one of the provided EndpointSlices is\n// managed by the EndpointSlice controller while the other is not.\nfunc (r *Reconciler) ManagedByChanged(endpointSlice1, endpointSlice2 *discovery.EndpointSlice) bool {\n\treturn r.ManagedByController(endpointSlice1) != r.ManagedByController(endpointSlice2)\n}\n\n// ManagedByController returns true if the controller of the provided\n// EndpointSlices is the EndpointSlice controller.\nfunc (r *Reconciler) runs a periodic loop to reconcile the desired state of the world with\n    46→// the actual state of the world by triggering attach detach operations.\n    47→// Note: This is distinct from the Reconciler implemented by the kubelet volume\n    48→// manager. This reconciles state for the attach/detach controller. That\n    49→// reconciles state for the kubelet volume manager.\n    50→type Reconciler interface {\n    51→\t// Starts running the reconciliation loop which executes periodically, checks\n    52→\t// if volumes that should be attached are attached and volumes that should\n    53→\t// be detached are detached. If not, it will trigger attach/detach\n    54→\t// operations to rectify.\n    55→\tRun(ctx context.Context)\n    56→}\n    57→\n    58→// NewReconciler returns a new instance of Reconciler that waits loopPeriod\n    59→// between successive executions.\n    60→// loopPeriod is the amount of time the reconciler loop waits between\n    61→// successive executions.\n    62→// maxWaitForUnmountDuration is the max amount of time the reconciler will wait\n    63→// for the volume to be safely unmounted, after this it will detach the volume\n    64→// anyway (to handle crashed/unavailable nodes). If during this time the volume\n    65→// becomes used by a new pod, the detach request will be aborted and the timer\n    66→// cleared.\n    67→func NewReconciler(\n    68→\tloopPeriod time.Duration,\n    69→\tmaxWaitForUnmountDuration time.Duration,\n    70→\tsyncDuration time.Duration,\n    71→\tdisableReconciliationSync bool,\n    72→\tdisableForceDetachOnTimeout bool,\n    73→\tdesiredStateOfWorld cache.DesiredStateOfWorld,\n    74→\tactualStateOfWorld cache.ActualStateOfWorld,\n    75→\tattacherDetacher operationexecutor.OperationExecutor,\n    76→\tnodeStatusUpdater   loopPeriod,\n    81→\t\tmaxWaitForUnmountDuration:   maxWaitForUnmountDuration,\n    82→\t\tsyncDuration:                syncDuration,\n    83→\t\tdisableReconciliationSync:   disableReconciliationSync,\n    84→\t\tdisableForceDetachOnTimeout: disableForceDetachOnTimeout,\n    85→\t\tdesiredStateOfWorld:         desiredStateOfWorld,\n    86→\t\tactualStateOfWorld: 90→\t\ttimeOfLastSync:              time.Now(),\n    91→\t\trecorder:                    recorder,\n    92→\t}\n    93→}\n    94→\n    95→type reconciler struct {\n    96→\tloopPeriod                  time.Duration\n    97→\tmaxWaitForUnmountDuration   time.Duration\n    98→\tsyncDuration                time.Duration\n    99→\tdesiredStateOfWorld         cache.DesiredStateOfWorld\n   100→\tactualStateOfWorld          cache.ActualStateOfWorld\n   101→\tattacherDetacher            operationexecutor.OperationExecutor\n   102→\tnodeStatusUpdater           statusupdater.NodeStatusUpdater\n   103→\tnodeLister                  corelisters.NodeLister\n   104→\ttimeOfLastSync              time.Time\n   105→\tdisableReconciliationSync   bool\n   106→\tdisableForceDetachOnTimeout bool\n   107→\trecorder                    record.EventRecorder\n   108→}\n   109→\n   110→func (rc *reconciler) Run(ctx context.Context) {\n   111→\twait.UntilWithContext(ctx, rc.reconciliationLoopFunc(ctx), rc.loopPeriod)\n   112→}\n   113→\n   114→// reconciliationLoopFunc this can be disabled via cli option disableReconciliation.\n   115→// It periodically checks whether the attached volumes from actual state\n   116→// are still attached to the node and update the status if they are not.\n   117→func (rc *reconciler) reconciliationLoopFunc(ctx context.Context) func(context.Context) {\n   118→\treturn func(ctx context.Context) {\n   119→\n   120→\t\trc.reconcile(ctx)\n   121→\t\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n   122→\t\tif rc.disableReconciliationSync {\n   123→\t\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"Skipping reconciling attached volumes still attached since it is disabled via the command line\")\n   124→\t\t} else if rc.syncDuration < time.Second {\n   125→\t\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"Skipping reconciling attached volumes still attached since it is set to less than one second via the command line\")\n   126→\t\t} else if time.Since(rc.timeOfLastSync) > rc.syncDuration {\n   127→\t\t\tlogger.V(5).Info(\"Starting reconciling attached volumes still attached\")\n   128→\t\t\trc.sync()\n   129→\t\t}\n   130→\t}\n   131→}\n   132→\n   133→func (rc *reconciler) sync() {\n   134→\tdefer rc.updateSyncTime()\n   135→\trc.syncStates()\n   136→}\n   137→\n   138→func (rc *reconciler) updateSyncTime() {\n   139→\trc.timeOfLastSync = time.Now()\n   140→}\n   141→\n   142→func (rc *reconciler) syncStates() {\n   143→\tvolumesPerNode := rc.actualStateOfWorld.GetAttachedVolumesPerNode()\n   144→\trc.attacherDetacher.VerifyVolumesAreAttached(volumesPerNode, rc.actualStateOfWorld)\n   145→}\n   146→\n   147→// hasOutOfServiceTaint returns true if the node has out-of-service taint present.\n   148→func (rc *reconciler) hasOutOfServiceTaint(nodeName types.NodeName) (bool, error) {\n   149→\tnode, err := rc.nodeLister.Get(string(nodeName))\n   150→\tif err != nil {\n   151→\t\treturn false, err\n   152→\t}\n   153→\treturn taints.TaintKeyExists(node.Spec.Taints, v1.TaintNodeOutOfService), nil\n   154→}\n   155→\n   156→// nodeIsHealthy returns true if the node looks healthy.\n   157→func (rc *reconciler) nodeIsHealthy(nodeName types.NodeName) (bool, error) {\n   158→\tnode, err := rc.nodeLister.Get(string(nodeName))\n   159→\tif err != nil {\n   160→\t\treturn false, err\n   161→\t}\n   162→\treturn nodeutil.IsNodeReady(node), nil\n   163→}\n   164→\n   165→func (rc *reconciler) reconcile(ctx context.Context) {\n   166→\t// Detaches are triggered before attaches so that volumes referenced by\n   167→\t// pods that are rescheduled to a different node are detached first.\n   168→\n   169→\t// Ensure volumes that should be detached are detached.\n   170→\tlogger := klog.FromContext(ctx)\n   171→\tfor _, attachedVolume := range rc.actualStateOfWorld.GetAttachedVolumes() {\n   172→\t\tif !rc.desiredStateOfWorld.VolumeExists(\n   173→\t\t\tattachedVolume.VolumeName, attachedVolume.NodeName) {\n   174→\n   175→\t\t\t// Check whether there already exist an operation pending, and don't even\n   176→\t\t\t// try to start an operation if there is already one running.\n   177→\t\t\t// This check must be done before we do any other checks, as otherwise the other checks\n   178→\t\t\t// may pass while at the same time the volume leaves the pending state, resulting in\n   179→\t\t\t// double detach attempts\n   180→\t\t\t// The operation key format is different depending on whether the volume\n   181→\t\t\t// allows multi attach across different nodes.\n   182→\t\t\tif util.IsMultiAttachAllowed(attachedVolume.VolumeSpec) {\n   183→\t\t\t\tif !rc.attacherDetacher.IsOperationSafeToRetry(attachedVolume.VolumeName, \"\" /* podName */, attachedVolume.NodeName, operationexecutor.DetachOperationName) {\n   184→\t\t\t\t\tlogger.V(10).Info(\"Operation for volume is already running or still in exponential backoff for node. Can't start detach\", \"node\", klog.KRef(\"\", string(attachedVolume.NodeName)), \"volumeName\", attachedVolume.VolumeName)\n   185→\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   186→\t\t\t\t}\n   187→\t\t\t} else {\n   188→\t\t\t\tif !rc.attacherDetacher.IsOperationSafeToRetry(attachedVolume.VolumeName, \"\" /* podName */, \"\" /* nodeName */, operationexecutor.DetachOperationName) {\n   189→\t\t\t\t\tlogger.V(10).Info(\"Operation for volume is already running or still in exponential backoff in the cluster. Can't start detach for node\", \"node\", klog.KRef(\"\", string(attachedVolume.NodeName)), \"volumeName\", attachedVolume.VolumeName)\n   190→\t\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   191→\t\t\t\t}\n   192→\t\t\t}\n volumeToAttach cache.VolumeToAttach, nodes []types.NodeName) {\n   373→\t// Filter out the current node from list of nodes where the volume is\n   374→\t// attached.\n   375→\t// Some methods need Typically\n   402→\t// it's user error, e.g. a ReplicaSet uses a PVC and has >1 replicas. Let\n   403→\t// the user know what pods are blocking the volume.\n   404→\tfor _, scheduledPod := range volumeToAttach.ScheduledPods {\n   405→\t\t// Each scheduledPod must get a custom message. They can run in\n   406→\t\t// different namespaces and user of a namespace should not see names of\n   407→\t\t// pods in other namespaces.\n   408→\t\tlocalPodNames := []string{} // Names of pods in scheduledPods's namespace\n   409→\t\totherPods := 0              // Count of pods in other namespaces\n   410→\t\tfor _, pod := range pods {\n   411→\t\t\tif pod.Namespace == scheduledPod.Namespace {\n   412→\t\t\t\tlocalPodNames = append(localPodNames, pod.Name)\n   413→\t\t\t} else {\n   414→\t\t\t\totherPods++\n   415→\t\t\t}\n   416→\t\t}\n   417→\n   418→\t\tvar msg string\n   419→\t\tif len(localPodNames) > 0 {\n   420→\t\t\tmsg = fmt.Sprintf(\"Volume is already used by pod(s) %s\", strings.Join(localPodNames, \", \"))\n   421→\t\t\tif otherPods > 0 {\n   422→\t\t\t\tmsg = fmt.Sprintf(\"%s and %d pod(s) in different namespaces\", msg, otherPods)\n   423→\t\t\t}\n   424→\t\t} else {\n   425→\t\t\t// No local pods, there are pods only in different namespaces.\n   426→\t\t\tmsg = fmt.Sprintf(\"Volume is already used by %d pod(s) in different namespaces\", otherPods)\n   427→\t\t}\n   428→\t\tsimpleMsg, _ := volumeToAttach.GenerateMsg(\"Multi-Attach error\", msg)\n   429→\t\trc.recorder.Eventf(scheduledPod, v1.EventTypeWarning, kevents.FailedAttachVolume, simpleMsg)\n   430→\t}\n   431→\n   432→\t// Log all pods for system admin\n   433→\tlogger.Info(\"Multi-Attach error: volume is already used by pods\", \"pods\", klog.KObjSlice(pods), \"attachedTo\", otherNodesStr, \"volume\", volumeToAttach)\n   434→}\n   435→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. *corev1.Service, pods []*corev1.Pod, existingSlices []*discovery.EndpointSlice, triggerTime time.Time) error {\n    84→\tslicesToDelete := []*discovery.EndpointSlice{} from topology cache\", \"existingSlice\", existingSlice, \"err\", err)\n   102→\t\t\t\t} else {\n   103→\t\t\t\t\tr.topologyCache.RemoveHints(svcKey, existingSlice.AddressType)\n   104→\t\t\t\t}\n   105→\t\t\t}\n   106→\n   107→\t\t\tslicesToDelete = append(slicesToDelete, existingSlice)\n   108→\t\t\tcontinue\n   109→\t\t}\n   110→\n   111→\t\t// add list if it is not on our map\n   112→\t\tif _, ok := slicesByAddressType[existingSlice.AddressType]; !ok {\n   113→\t\t\tslicesByAddressType[existingSlice.AddressType] = make([]*discovery.EndpointSlice, 0, 1)\n   114→\t\t}\n   115→\n   116→\t\tslicesByAddressType[existingSlice.AddressType] = append(slicesByAddressType[existingSlice.AddressType], existingSlice)\n   117→\t}\n   118→\n   119→\t// reconcile for existing.\n   120→\tfor addressType := range serviceSupportedAddressesTypes {\n   121→\t\texistingSlices := slicesByAddressType[addressType]\n   122→\t\terr := r.reconcileByAddressType(logger, service, pods, existingSlices, triggerTime, addressType)\n   123→\t\tif err != nil {\n   124→\t\t\terrs = append(errs, err)\n   125→\t\t}\n   126→\t}\n   127→\n   128→\t// delete those which are of addressType that is no longer supported\n   129→\t// by the service\n   130→\tfor _, sliceToDelete := range slicesToDelete {\n   131→\t\terr := r.client.DiscoveryV1().EndpointSlices(service.Namespace).Delete(context.TODO(), sliceToDelete.Name, metav1.DeleteOptions{})\n   132→\t\tif err != nil {\n   133→\t\t\terrs = append(errs, fmt.Errorf(\"error deleting %s EndpointSlice for Service %s/%s: %w\", sliceToDelete.Name, service.Namespace, service.Name, err))\n   134→\t\t} else {\n   135→\t\t\tr.endpointSliceTracker.ExpectDeletion(sliceToDelete)\n   136→\t\t\tmetrics.EndpointSliceChanges.WithLabelValues(\"delete\").Inc()\n   137→\t\t}\n   138→\t}\n   139→\n   140→\treturn utilerrors.NewAggregate(errs)\n   141→}\n   142→\n   143→// reconcileByAddressType takes a set of pods currently matching a service selector and\n   144→// compares them with the endpoints already present in any existing endpoint\n   145→// slices (by address type) for the given service. It creates, updates, or deletes endpoint slices\n   146→// to ensure the desired set of pods are represented by endpoint slices.\n   147→func (r *Reconciler) reconcileByAddressType(logger klog.Logger, service *corev1.Service, pods []*corev1.Pod, existingSlices []*discovery.EndpointSlice, triggerTime time.Time, addressType discovery.AddressType) error {\n   148→\terrs := []error{}\n   149→\n   150→\tslicesToCreate := []*discovery.EndpointSlice{}\n   151→\tslicesToUpdate := []*discovery.EndpointSlice{}\n   152→\tslicesToDelete := []*discovery.EndpointSlice{}\n   153→\tevents := []*topologycache.EventBuilder{}\n   154→\n   155→\t// Build data structures for existing state.\n   156→\texistingSlicesByPortMap := map[endpointsliceutil.PortMapKey][]*discovery.EndpointSlice{}\n   157→\tfor _, existingSlice := range existingSlices {\n   158→\t\tif ownedBy(existingSlice, service) {\n   159→\t\t\tepHash := endpointsliceutil.NewPortMapKey(existingSlice.Ports)\n   160→\t\t\texistingSlicesByPortMap[epHash] = append(existingSlicesByPortMap[epHash], existingSlice)\n   161→\t\t} else {\n   162→\t\t\tslicesToDelete = append(slicesToDelete, existingSlice)\n   163→\t\t}\n   164→\t}\n   165→\n   166→\t// Build data structures for desired state.\n   167→\tdesiredMetaByPortMap := map[endpointsliceutil.PortMapKey]*endpointMeta{}\n   168→\tdesiredEndpointsByPortMap := map[endpointsliceutil.PortMapKey]endpointsliceutil.EndpointSet{}\n   169→\n   170→\tfor _, pod := range pods {\n   171→\t\tif !endpointsliceutil.ShouldPodBeInEndpoints(pod, true) {\n   172→\t\t\tcontinue\n   173→\t\t}\n   174→\n   175→\t\tendpointPorts := getEndpointPorts(logger, service, pod)\n   176→\t\tepHash := endpointsliceutil.NewPortMapKey(endpointPorts)\n   177→\t\tif _, ok := desiredEndpointsByPortMap[epHash]; !ok {\n   178→\t\t\tdesiredEndpointsByPortMap[epHash] = endpointsliceutil.EndpointSet{}\n   179→\t\t}\n   180→\n   181→\t\tif _, ok := desiredMetaByPortMap[epHash]; !ok {\n   182→\t\t\tdesiredMetaByPortMap[epHash] = &endpointMeta{\n   183→\t\t\t\taddressType: addressType,\n   184→\t\t\t\tports:       endpointPorts,\n   185→\t\t\t}\n   186→\t\t}\n   187→\n   188→\t\tnode, err := r.nodeLister.Get(pod.Spec.NodeName)\n   189→\t\tif err != nil {\n   190→\t\t\t// we are getting the information from the local informer,\n   191→\t\t\t// an error different than IsNotFound should not happen\n   192→\t\t\tif !errors.IsNotFound(err) {\n   193→\t\t\t\treturn err\n   194→\t\t\t}\n   195→\t\t\t// If the Node specified by the Pod doesn't exist we want to requeue the Service so we\n   196→\t\t\t// retry later, but also update the EndpointSlice without the problematic Pod.\n   197→\t\t\t// Theoretically, the pod Garbage Collector will remove the Pod, but we want to avoid\n   198→\t\t\t// situations where a reference from a Pod to a missing node can leave the EndpointSlice\n   199→\t\t\t// stuck forever.\n   200→\t\t\t// On the other side, if the service.Spec.PublishNotReadyAddresses is set we just add the\n   201→\t\t\t// Pod, since the user is explicitly indicating that the Pod address should be published.\n   202→\t\t\tif !service.Spec.PublishNotReadyAddresses {\n   203→\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"skipping Pod for Service, Node not found\", \"pod\", klog.KObj(pod), \"service\", klog.KObj(service), \"node\", klog.KRef(\"\", pod.Spec.NodeName))\n   204→\t\t\t\terrs = append(errs, fmt.Errorf(\"skipping Pod %s for Service %s/%s: Node %s Not Found\", pod.Name, service.Namespace, service.Name, pod.Spec.NodeName))\n   205→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   206→\t\t\t}\n   207→\t\t}\n   208→\t\tendpoint := podToEndpoint(pod, node, service, addressType)\n   209→\t\tif len(endpoint.Addresses) > 0 {\n   210→\t\t\tdesiredEndpointsByPortMap[epHash].Insert(&endpoint)\n   211→\t\t}\n   212→\t}\n   213→\n   214→\tspMetrics := metrics.NewServicePortCache()\n   215→\ttotalAdded := 0\n   216→\ttotalRemoved := 0\n   217→\n   218→\t// Determine changes necessary for each group of slices by port map.\n   219→\tfor portMap, desiredEndpoints := range desiredEndpointsByPortMap {\n   220→\t\tnumEndpoints := len(desiredEndpoints)\n   221→\t\tpmSlicesToCreate, pmSlicesToUpdate, pmSlicesToDelete, added, removed := r.reconcileByPortMapping(\n   222→\t\t\tlogger, service, existingSlicesByPortMap[portMap], desiredEndpoints, desiredMetaByPortMap[portMap])\n   223→\n   224→\t\ttotalAdded += added\n   225→\t\ttotalRemoved += removed\n   226→\n   227→\t\tspMetrics.Set(portMap, metrics.EfficiencyInfo{\n   228→\t\t\tEndpoints: numEndpoints,\n   229→\t\t\tSlices:    len(existingSlicesByPortMap[portMap]) + len(pmSlicesToCreate) - len(pmSlicesToDelete),\n   230→\t\t})\n   231→\n   232→\t\tslicesToCreate = append(slicesToCreate, pmSlicesToCreate...)\n   233→\t\tslicesToUpdate = append(slicesToUpdate, pmSlicesToUpdate...)\n   234→\t\tslicesToDelete = append(slicesToDelete, pmSlicesToDelete...)\n   235→\t}\n   236→\n   237→\t// If there are unique sets of ports that are no longer desired, mark\n   238→\t// the corresponding endpoint slices for deletion.\n   239→\tfor portMap, existingSlices := range existingSlicesByPortMap {\n   240→\t\tif _, ok := desiredEndpointsByPortMap[portMap]; !ok {\n   241→\t\t\tslicesToDelete = append(slicesToDelete, existingSlices...)\n   242→\t\t}\n   243→\t}\n   244→\n   245→\t// When no endpoint slices would usually exist, we need to add a placeholder.\n   246→\tif len(existingSlices) == len(slicesToDelete) && len(slicesToCreate) < 1 {\n   247→\t\t// Check for existing placeholder slice outside of the core control flow\n   248→\t\tplaceholderSlice := newEndpointSlice(logger, service, &endpointMeta{ports: []discovery.EndpointPort{}, addressType: addressType}, r.controllerName)\n   249→\t\tif len(slicesToDelete) == 1 && placeholderSliceCompare.DeepEqual(slicesToDelete[0], placeholderSlice) {\n   250→\t\t\t// We are about to unnecessarily delete/recreate the placeholder, remove it now.\n   251→\t\t\tslicesToDelete = slicesToDelete[:0]\n   252→\t\t} else {\n   253→\t\t\tslicesToCreate = append(slicesToCreate, placeholderSlice)\n   254→\t\t}\n   255→\t\tspMetrics.Set(endpointsliceutil.NewPortMapKey(placeholderSlice.Ports), metrics.EfficiencyInfo{\n   256→\t\t\tEndpoints: 0,\n   257→\t\t\tSlices:    1,\n   258→\t\t})\n   259→\t}\n   260→\n   261→\tmetrics.EndpointsAddedPerSync.WithLabelValues().Observe(float64(totalAdded))\n   262→\tmetrics.EndpointsRemovedPerSync.WithLabelValues().Observe(float64(totalRemoved))\n   263→\n   264→\tserviceNN := types.NamespacedName{Name: service.Name, Namespace: service.Namespace}\n   265→\tr.metricsCache.UpdateServicePortCache(serviceNN, spMetrics)\n   266→\n   267→\t// Topology hints are assigned per address type. This means it is\n   268→\t// theoretically possible for endpoints of one address type to be assigned\n   269→\t// hints while another endpoints of another address type are not.\n   270→\tsi := &topologycache.SliceInfo{\n   271→\t\tServiceKey:  fmt.Sprintf(\"%s/%s\", service.Namespace, service.Name),\n   272→\t\tAddressType: addressType,\n   273→\t\tToCreate:    slicesToCreate,\n   274→\t\tToUpdate:    slicesToUpdate,\n   275→\t\tUnchanged:   unchangedSlices(existingSlices, slicesToUpdate, slicesToDelete),\n   276→\t}\n   277→\n   278→\tcanUseTrafficDistribution := r.trafficDistributionEnabled && !hintsEnabled(service.Annotations)\n   279→\n   280→\t// Check if we need to add/remove hints based on the topology annotation.\n   281→\t//\n   282→\t// This if/else clause can be removed once the annotation has been deprecated.\n   283→\t// Ref: https://github.com/kubernetes/enhancements/tree/master/keps/sig-network/4444-service-routing-preference\n   284→\tif r.topologyCache != nil && hintsEnabled(service.Annotations) {\n   285→\t\t// Reaching this point means that we need to configure hints based on the\n   286→\t\t// topology annotation.\n   287→\t\tslicesToCreate, slicesToUpdate, events = r.topologyCache.AddHints(logger, si)\n   288→\n   289→\t} else {\n   290→\t\t// Reaching this point means that we will not be configuring hints based on\n   291→\t\t// the topology annotation. We need to do 2 things:\n   292→\t\t//  1. If hints were added previously based on the annotation, we need to\n   293→\t\t//     clear up any locally cached hints from the topologyCache object.\n   294→\t\t//  2. Optionally remove the actual hints from the EndpointSlice if we know\n   295→\t\t//     that the `trafficDistribution` field is also NOT being used. In other\n   296→\t\t//     words, if we know that the `trafficDistribution` field has been\n   297→\t\t//     correctly configured by the customer, we DO NOT remove the hints and\n   298→\t\t//     wait for the trafficDist handlers to correctly configure them. Always\n   299→\t\t//     unconditionally removing hints here (and letting them get readded by\n   300→\t\t//     the trafficDist) adds extra overhead in the form of DeepCopy (done\n   301→\t\t//     within topologyCache.RemoveHints)\n   302→\n   303→\t\t// Check 1.\n   304→\t\tif r.topologyCache != nil {\n   305→\t\t\tif r.topologyCache.HasPopulatedHints(si.ServiceKey) {\n   306→\t\t\t\tlogger.Info(\"TopologyAwareHints annotation has changed, removing hints\", \"serviceKey\", si.ServiceKey, \"addressType\", si.AddressType)\n   307→\t\t\t\tevents = append(events, &topologycache.EventBuilder{\n   308→\t\t\t\t\tEventType: corev1.EventTypeWarning,\n   309→\t\t\t\t\tReason:    \"TopologyAwareHintsDisabled\",\n   310→\t\t\t\t\tMessage:   topologycache.FormatWithAddressType(topologycache.TopologyAwareHintsDisabled, si.AddressType),\n   311→\t\t\t\t})\n   312→\t\t\t}\n   313→\t\t\tr.topologyCache.RemoveHints(si.ServiceKey, addressType)\n   314→\t\t}\n   315→\n   316→\t\t// Check 2.\n   317→\t\tif !canUseTrafficDistribution {\n   318→\t\t\tslicesToCreate, slicesToUpdate = topologycache.RemoveHintsFromSlices(si)\n   319→\t\t}\n   320→\t}\n   321→\n   322→\tif canUseTrafficDistribution {\n   323→\t\tr.metricsCache.UpdateTrafficDistributionForService(serviceNN, service.Spec.TrafficDistribution)\n   324→\t\tslicesToCreate, slicesToUpdate, _ = trafficdist.ReconcileHints(service.Spec.TrafficDistribution, slicesToCreate, slicesToUpdate, unchangedSlices(existingSlices, slicesToUpdate, slicesToDelete))\n   325→\t} else {\n   326→\t\tr.metricsCache.UpdateTrafficDistributionForService(serviceNN, nil)\n   327→\t}\n   328→\n   329→\terr := r.finalize(service, slicesToCreate, slicesToUpdate, slicesToDelete, triggerTime)\n   330→\tif err != nil {\n   331→\t\terrs = append(errs, err)\n   332→\t}\n   333→\tfor _, event := range events {\n   334→\t\tr.eventRecorder.Event(service, event.EventType, event.Reason, event.Message)\n   335→\t}\n   336→\treturn utilerrors.NewAggregate(errs)\n   337→\n   338→}\n   339→\n   340→func NewReconciler(client clientset.Interface, nodeLister corelisters.NodeLister, maxEndpointsPerSlice int32, endpointSliceTracker *endpointsliceutil.EndpointSliceTracker, topologyCache *topologycache.TopologyCache, eventRecorder record.EventRecorder, controllerName string, options ...ReconcilerOption) *Reconciler {\n   341→\tr := &Reconciler{\n   342→\t\tclient:               client,\n   343→\t\tnodeLister:           nodeLister,\n   344→\t\tmaxEndpointsPerSlice: maxEndpointsPerSlice,\n   345→\t\tendpointSliceTracker: endpointSliceTracker,\n   346→\t\tmetricsCache:         metrics.NewCache(maxEndpointsPerSlice),\n   347→\t\ttopologyCache:        topologyCache,\n   348→\t\teventRecorder:        eventRecorder,\n   349→\t\tcontrollerName:       controllerName,\n   350→\t}\n   351→\tfor _, option := range options {\n   352→\t\toption(r)\n   353→\t}\n   354→\treturn r\n   355→}\n   356→\n   357→// placeholderSliceCompare is a conversion func for comparing two placeholder endpoint slices.\n   358→// It only compares the specific fields we care about.\n   359→var placeholderSliceCompare = conversion.EqualitiesOrDie(\n   360→\tfunc(a, b metav1.OwnerReference) bool {\n   361→\t\treturn a.String() == b.String()\n   362→\t},\n   363→\tfunc(a, b metav1.ObjectMeta) bool {\n   364→\t\tif a.Namespace != b.Namespace {\n   365→\t\t\treturn false\n   366→\t\t}\n   367→\t\tfor k, v := range a.Labels {\n   368→\t\t\tif b.Labels[k] != v {\n   369→\t\t\t\treturn false\n   370→\t\t\t}\n   371→\t\t}\n   372→\t\tfor k, v := range b.Labels {\n   373→\t\t\tif a.Labels[k] != v {\n   374→\t\t\t\treturn false\n   375→\t\t\t}\n   376→\t\t}\n   377→\t\treturn true\n   378→\t},\n   379→)\n   380→\n   381→// finalize creates, updates, and deletes slices as specified\n   382→func (r *Reconciler) finalize(\n   383→\tservice *corev1.Service,\n   384→\tslicesToCreate,\n   385→\tslicesToUpdate,\n   386→\tslicesToDelete []*discovery.EndpointSlice,\n   387→\ttriggerTime time.Time,\n   388→) error {\n   389→\t// If there are slices to create and delete, change the creates to updates\n   390→\t// of the slices that would otherwise be deleted.\n   391→\tfor i := 0; i < len(slicesToDelete); {\n   392→\t\tif len(slicesToCreate) == 0 {\n   393→\t\t\tbreak\n   394→\t\t}\n   395→\t\tsliceToDelete := slicesToDelete[i]\n   396→\t\tslice := slicesToCreate[len(slicesToCreate)-1]\n   397→\t\t// Only update EndpointSlices that are owned by this Service and have\n   398→\t\t// the same AddressType. We need to avoid updating EndpointSlices that\n   399→\t\t// are being garbage collected for an old Service with the same name.\n   400→\t\t// The AddressType field is immutable. Since Services also consider\n   401→\t\t// IPFamily immutable, the only case where this should matter will be\n   402→\t\t// the migration from IP to IPv4 and IPv6 AddressTypes, where there's a\n   403→\t\t// chance EndpointSlices with an IP AddressType would otherwise be\n   404→\t\t// updated to IPv4 or IPv6 without this check.\n   405→\t\tif sliceToDelete.AddressType == slice.AddressType && ownedBy(sliceToDelete, service) {\n   406→\t\t\tslice.Name = sliceToDelete.Name\n   407→\t\t\tslicesToCreate = slicesToCreate[:len(slicesToCreate)-1]\n   408→\t\t\tslicesToUpdate = append(slicesToUpdate, slice)\n   409→\t\t\tslicesToDelete = append(slicesToDelete[:i], slicesToDelete[i+1:]...)\n   410→\t\t} else {\n   411→\t\t\ti++\n   412→\t\t}\n   413→\t}\n   414→\n   415→\t// Don't create new EndpointSlices if the Service is pending deletion. This\n   416→\t// is to avoid a potential race condition with the garbage collector where\n   417→\t// it tries to delete EndpointSlices as this controller replaces them.\n   418→\tif service.DeletionTimestamp == nil {\n   419→\t\tfor _, endpointSlice := range slicesToCreate {\n   420→\t\t\taddTriggerTimeAnnotation(endpointSlice, triggerTime)\n   421→\t\t\tcreatedSlice, err := r.client.DiscoveryV1().EndpointSlices(service.Namespace).Create(context.TODO(), endpointSlice, metav1.CreateOptions{})\n   422→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   423→\t\t\t\t// If the namespace is terminating, creates will continue to fail. Simply drop the item.\n   424→\t\t\t\tif errors.HasStatusCause(err, corev1.NamespaceTerminatingCause) {\n   425→\t\t\t\t\treturn nil\n   426→\t\t\t\t}\n   427→\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to create EndpointSlice for Service %s/%s: %v\", service.Namespace, service.Name, err)\n   428→\t\t\t}\n   429→\t\t\tr.endpointSliceTracker.Update(createdSlice)\n   430→\t\t\tmetrics.EndpointSliceChanges.WithLabelValues(\"create\").Inc()\n   431→\t\t}\n   432→\t}\n   433→\n   434→\tfor _, endpointSlice := range slicesToUpdate {\n   435→\t\taddTriggerTimeAnnotation(endpointSlice, triggerTime)\n   436→\t\tupdatedSlice, err := r.client.DiscoveryV1().EndpointSlices(service.Namespace).Update(context.TODO(), endpointSlice, metav1.UpdateOptions{})\n   437→\t\tif err != nil {\n   438→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to update %s EndpointSlice for Service %s/%s: %v\", endpointSlice.Name, service.Namespace, service.Name, err)\n   439→\t\t}\n   440→\t\tr.endpointSliceTracker.Update(updatedSlice)\n   441→\t\tmetrics.EndpointSliceChanges.WithLabelValues(\"update\").Inc()\n   442→\t}\n   443→\n   444→\tfor _, endpointSlice := range slicesToDelete {\n   445→\t\terr := r.client.DiscoveryV1().EndpointSlices(service.Namespace).Delete(context.TODO(), endpointSlice.Name, metav1.DeleteOptions{})\n   446→\t\tif err != nil {\n   447→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"failed to delete %s EndpointSlice for Service %s/%s: %v\", endpointSlice.Name, service.Namespace, service.Name, err)\n   448→\t\t}\n   449→\t\tr.endpointSliceTracker.ExpectDeletion(endpointSlice)\n   450→\t\tmetrics.EndpointSliceChanges.WithLabelValues(\"delete\").Inc()\n   451→\t}\n   452→\n   453→\ttopologyLabel := \"Disabled\"\n   454→\tif r.topologyCache != nil && hintsEnabled(service.Annotations) {\n   455→\t\ttopologyLabel = \"Auto\"\n   456→\t}\n   457→\tvar trafficDistribution string\n   458→\tif r.trafficDistributionEnabled && !hintsEnabled(service.Annotations) {\n   459→\t\tif service.Spec.TrafficDistribution != nil && *service.Spec.TrafficDistribution == corev1.ServiceTrafficDistributionPreferClose {\n   460→\t\t\ttrafficDistribution = *service.Spec.TrafficDistribution\n   461→\t\t}\n   462→\t}\n   463→\n   464→\tnumSlicesChanged := len(slicesToCreate) + len(slicesToUpdate) + len(slicesToDelete)\n   465→\tmetrics.EndpointSlicesChangedPerSync.WithLabelValues(topologyLabel, trafficDistribution).Observe(float64(numSlicesChanged))\n   466→\n   467→\treturn nil\n   468→}\n   469→\n   470→// reconcileByPortMapping compares the endpoints found in existing slices with\n   471→// the list of desired endpoints and returns lists of slices to create, update,\n   472→// and delete. It also checks that the slices mirror the parent services labels.\n   473→// The logic is split up into several main steps:\n   474→//  1. Iterate through existing slices, delete endpoints that are no longer\n   475→//     desired and update matching endpoints that have changed. It also checks\n   476→//     if the slices have the labels of the parent services, and updates them if not.\n   477→//  2. Iterate through slices that have been modified in 1 and fill them up with\n   478→//     any remaining desired endpoints.\n   479→//  3. If there still desired endpoints left, try to fit them into a previously\n   480→//     unchanged slice and/or create new ones.\n   481→func (r *Reconciler) reconcileByPortMapping(\n   482→\tlogger klog.Logger,\n   483→\tservice *corev1.Service,\n   484→\texistingSlices []*discovery.EndpointSlice,\n   485→\tdesiredSet endpointsliceutil.EndpointSet,\n   486→\tendpointMeta *endpointMeta,\n   487→) ([]*discovery.EndpointSlice, []*discovery.EndpointSlice, []*discovery.EndpointSlice, int, int) {\n   488→\tslicesByName := map[string]*discovery.EndpointSlice{}\n   489→\tsliceNamesUnchanged := sets.New[string]()\n   490→\tsliceNamesToUpdate := sets.New[string]()\n   491→\tsliceNamesToDelete := sets.New[string]()\n   492→\tnumRemoved := 0\n   493→\n   494→\t// 1. Iterate through existing slices to delete endpoints no longer desired\n   495→\t//    and update endpoints that have changed\n   496→\tfor _, existingSlice := range existingSlices {\n   497→\t\tslicesByName[existingSlice.Name] = existingSlice\n   498→\t\tnewEndpoints := []discovery.Endpoint{}\n   499→\t\tendpointUpdated := false\n   500→\t\tfor _, endpoint := range existingSlice.Endpoints {\n   501→\t\t\tgot := desiredSet.Get(&endpoint)\n   502→\t\t\t// If endpoint is desired add it to list of endpoints to keep.\n   503→\t\t\tif got != nil {\n   504→\t\t\t\tnewEndpoints = append(newEndpoints, *got)\n   505→\t\t\t\t// If existing version of endpoint doesn't match desired version\n   506→\t\t\t\t// set endpointUpdated to ensure endpoint changes are persisted.\n   507→\t\t\t\tif !endpointsliceutil.EndpointsEqualBeyondHash(got, &endpoint) {\n   508→\t\t\t\t\tendpointUpdated = true\n   509→\t\t\t\t}\n   510→\t\t\t\t// once an endpoint has been placed/found in a slice, it no\n   511→\t\t\t\t// longer needs to be handled\n   512→\t\t\t\tdesiredSet.Delete(&endpoint)\n   513→\t\t\t}\n   514→\t\t}\n   515→\n   516→\t\t// generate the slice labels and check if parent labels have changed\n   517→\t\tlabels, labelsChanged := setEndpointSliceLabels(logger, existingSlice, service, r.controllerName)\n   518→\n   519→\t\t// If an endpoint was updated or removed, mark for update or delete\n   520→\t\tif endpointUpdated || len(existingSlice.Endpoints) != len(newEndpoints) {\n   521→\t\t\tif len(existingSlice.Endpoints) > len(newEndpoints) {\n   522→\t\t\t\tnumRemoved += len(existingSlice.Endpoints) -
